UX RESEARCH DOCUMENTS & FINDINGS\n\n### 2.1 Competitor Analysis (ux-competitor-analysis.md - 318 lines)\n\n**Three main competitors analyzed:**\n\n#### IBM Maximo Scheduler\n- **Strength**: Drag-drop Gantt + resource histogram (gold standard)\n- **Weakness**: Struggles at 10k+ records; discrete day/week/month tabs\n- **Steal**: Drag-drop capability, resource loading visualization\n\n#### Railnova (Brussels-based)\n- **Strength**: Event state pipeline (unplanned → planned → overdue → closed)\n- **Strength**: Digital train logbook for drivers/technicians\n- **Strength**: Color-coded anomaly detection\n- **Steal**: Event state machine, anomaly indicators, real-time monitoring\n\n#### SignatureRail (TrainPlan since 1994)\n- **Strength**: Marey chart visualization (industry gold standard since 1878)\n- **Strength**: What-if scenario management\n- **Marey advantage**: Superior time/space visualization for train scheduling\n- **Steal**: Marey chart implementation, scenario comparison\n\n**Gestalt Principles Applied:**\n- Proximity: Group related filters near views\n- Similarity: Consistent colors for data types\n- Enclosure: Cards with clear borders\n- Connectedness: Dependency lines between tasks\n- Closure: Minimal axis lines\n- Continuity: Chronological sorting\n\n**Differentiators:**\n| Feature | Competitors | MMS |\n|---------|-------------|-----|\n| Zoom | Discrete tabs | Continuous semantic zoom |\n| Performance | Struggles @ 10k | 60fps @ 60k tasks |\n| Interface | Fragmented modules | Unified canvas |\n| Visualization | Gantt only | Gantt + Marey + Heatmap (LOD) |\n\n### 2.2 Unknown Unknowns (ux-unknown-unknowns.md - 387 lines)\n\n**10 Critical Domain Discoveries:**\n\n1. **Statutory Tasks** (Non-moveable)\n   - Government-mandated safety inspections cannot be rescheduled\n   - UX: Lock icon + striped pattern\n   - Add to Task type: `isStatutory: boolean`\n\n2. **Depot Bay Limits** (Physical constraint)\n   - Al Rashidiya: 4-6 bays (49 Kinki Sharyo trains)\n   - Jebel Ali: 6-8 bays (79 Alstom trains)\n   - Cannot schedule more trains than bays available\n   - Need: Bay conflict detection (different from time conflicts)\n\n3. **Dependency Bottleneck** (Cascading changes)\n   - Moving one task can affect 12+ dependent tasks\n   - Performance: Cannot recalculate on every drag\n   - Solution: Debounced impact calculation (300ms), progressive disclosure\n\n4. **24-Hour Operation Reality**\n   - Maintenance windows: 5-6 hours/night (12:00am - 5:30am)\n   - Some special events: 24hr operation\n   - Need: Maintenance window visualization on timeline\n\n5. **Disruption Mode** (Disaster recovery)\n   - Dubai flooding (Apr 2024) closed stations for 38 days\n   - Need: Emergency schedule activation, backlog tracking, recovery planning\n\n6. **Standardized KPIs** (EN 15341 standard)\n   - MTBF: Mean Time Between Failures (higher = better)\n   - MTTR: Mean Time To Repair (lower = better)\n   - PM Compliance: > 95%\n   - Schedule Compliance: > 90%\n   - Need: KPI dashboard with trends and drill-down\n\n7. **Approval Workflows** (Multi-level)\n   - Depot Manager approves weekly schedule changes\n   - Operations Director approves overhauls\n   - Finance approves resource changes\n   - Need: Role-based access, approval queue, audit trail\n\n8. **Spare Parts Availability** (#1 delay cause)\n   - #1 reason tasks don't happen: parts unavailable\n   - Need: Parts status indicator (Green/Yellow/Red by ETA)\n   - Integration point: SAP/Maximo for stock levels\n\n9. **Mobile for Technicians**\n   - Floor-level staff need tablet interface (Railnova Digital Train Logbook pattern)\n   - \"My tasks today\" view\n   - Offline capability (caching)\n   - Photo upload for issues\n\n10. **Historical Data for Predictions**\n    - Track actual vs estimated duration\n    - Build ML model for future predictions\n    - Show confidence intervals (\"±30min confidence\")\n    - Anomaly detection (\"Train X needs 3x normal maintenance\")\n\n**Priority Matrix:**\n- **Must Have (Phase 1)**: Statutory locks, Bay capacity, KPIs, Impact preview\n- **Should Have (Phase 1.5)**: Maintenance windows, Approval workflow, Disruption mode\n- **Nice to Have (Phase 2)**: Parts availability, Mobile view, AI predictions\n\n### 2.3 Design System (design-system.md - 560 lines)\n\n**Color Palette (Dark Theme Primary):**\n- `--mms-bg-app`: #1a1a2e (main background)\n- `--mms-bg-card`: #16213e (card/panel)\n- `--mms-text-primary`: #f9fafb (near white)\n- `--canvas-bg`: #0A0A0A (pure black - OLED power savings)\n- Maintenance types: PM1 (green), PM2 (blue), HM (amber), OVH (red)\n- Status: Available (green), In-service (blue), Maintenance (red)\n- Variance: Green (good), Yellow (warning), Red (danger)\n\n**Typography:**\n- Primary font: Inter\n- Monospace: JetBrains Mono (train IDs, timestamps)\n- Sizes: 10px (xs) → 36px (4xl)\n- Weights: 500 (medium), 600 (semibold)\n\n**Spacing (4px base unit):**\n- `--mms-sidebar-width`: 130px (collapsed), 280px (expanded)\n- `--mms-navbar-height`: 44px\n- `--px-per-train`: 24px\n- `--px-per-day`: 2px\n- `--task-card-height`: 36px\n\n**LOD System:**\n```\nZoom:  0.05  0.35  0.50         2.00  2.15  5.0\nMACRO  [=====|-----|             |     |    ]\nMESO         [-----|=============|-----|    ]\nMICRO        |     [-----|=============|====]\n```\n- MACRO: < 0.5 zoom (heatmap, 100% opacity)\n- MESO: 0.5-2.0 zoom (DNA/bars, 100% opacity)\n- MICRO: > 2.0 zoom (detailed cards, 100% opacity)\n- Crossfade zones: 15% hysteresis overlap\n\n**Three-Layer Sandwich Architecture:**\n```\nLayer 3: HUD Overlay (HTML/React) - pointer-events: none\n  └─ Navbar, Sidebar, Timeline Header, Minimap, Tooltips\nLayer 2: Canvas (WebGL/R3F)\n  └─ Task bars, dependency lines, heatmaps, LOD layers\nLayer 1: Engine\n  └─ Constraint processing, data calculations\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. DESIGN DECISIONS & PATTERNS\n\n### 3.1 Architecture Decision Records (architecture-decisions.md)\n\n**ADR-001: PixiJS v8 for WebGL** (NOT in final!)\n- **Rejected**: DOM/SVG rendering inadequate for 500k+ data points\n- **Choice**: PixiJS v8 (most performant 2D WebGL engine)\n- **Note**: Later evolved to React Three Fiber in final implementation\n\n**ADR-002: pixi-viewport for Navigation**\n- **Pattern**: Google Maps-style pan/zoom with inertia\n- **Physics**: Native smooth zoom, pinch-to-zoom, momentum\n- **Alternative**: Custom physics (too expensive)\n\n**ADR-003: Virtual Scrolling (Math-based)**\n- **Rejected**: Ghost Div Pattern (DOM scrolling)\n- **Rejected**: react-window, react-virtualized\n- **Choice**: Physics-based virtual scroller for seamless fractal zoom\n\n**ADR-004: Structure of Arrays (SoA) with TypedArrays**\n- **Pattern**: Separate Float64Array, Uint16Array per property\n- **Benefit**: Zero GC during interaction, cache locality\n- **Tradeoff**: Verbose code, harder debugging\n- **Code example**: `startMs: Float64Array`, `aircraftIndex: Uint16Array`\n\n**ADR-005: @belt/tools State Machine (NOT React Hooks)**\n- **Rejected**: useState/useRef/useEffect (stale closures)\n- **Rejected**: Zustand (mutable state issues)\n- **Choice**: @belt/tools with `useSyncExternalStore`\n- **Benefit**: Synchronous state access, works in animation loops\n\n**ADR-006: Vite SPA** (NOT Next.js)\n- **Rejected**: Astro, Next.js (no SSR needed)\n- **Choice**: Vite 6 for minimal, fast dev server\n\n### 3.2 Code Patterns (code-patterns.md - 60k lines of reference)\n\n**Working Pattern: External Store + useSyncExternalStore**\n\n```typescript\n// viewport.ts\nclass ViewportStore {\n  private state: ViewportState;\n  private listeners: Set<Listener>;\n  \n  getState = (): ViewportState => this.state;\n  subscribe = (listener: Listener) => { /* ... */ };\n  \n  pan = (dx: number, dy: number) => { /* update state */ };\n  zoomIn = () => { /* update state */ };\n}\n\nexport const viewportStore = new ViewportStore();\n\nexport function useViewport() {\n  const state = useSyncExternalStore(viewportStore.subscribe, viewportStore.getState);\n  return { state, actions: { pan, zoomIn, ... } };\n}\n```\n\n**Benefit**: State always synchronous, no stale closures, works in `useFrame` loops\n\n**Working Pattern: Structure of Arrays (SoA)**\n\n```typescript\n// mockData.ts\nexport interface TaskSoA {\n  count: number;\n  ids: string[];\n  trainIds: Uint16Array;      // Per-task train index\n  startDays: Uint32Array;     // Per-task start day\n  durations: Uint32Array;     // Per-task duration\n  types: Uint8Array;          // Per-task type (0=preventive, 1=corrective...)\n}\n\nexport function tasksToSoA(tasks: Task[]): TaskSoA {\n  const soa: TaskSoA = {\n    count: tasks.length,\n    ids: tasks.map(t => t.id),\n    trainIds: new Uint16Array(tasks.map(t => t.trainId)),\n    startDays: new Uint32Array(tasks.map(t => t.startDay)),\n    durations: new Uint32Array(tasks.map(t => t.duration)),\n    types: new Uint8Array(tasks.map(t => TASK_TYPE_INDEX[t.type])),\n  };\n  return soa;\n}\n```\n\n**Benefit**: Contiguous memory, fast iteration, minimal GC\n\n**Working Pattern: InstancedMesh for Rendering**\n\n```typescript\n// MesoLayer.tsx - Task blocks using InstancedMesh\nfunction TaskBlocks({ tasks, conflictIndices }: TaskBlocksProps) {\n  const meshRef = useRef<THREE.InstancedMesh>(null);\n  \n  const { matrices, colors } = useMemo(() => {\n    const matrices = new Float32Array(tasks.count * 16);\n    const colors = new Float32Array(tasks.count * 3);\n    \n    for (let i = 0; i < tasks.count; i++) {\n      // Position: x = startDay * DAY_WIDTH + width/2\n      const x = tasks.startDays[i]! * DAY_WIDTH + ...\n      // Color: conflict? red : task type color\n      const color = conflictIndices?.has(i) ? CONFLICT_COLOR : typeColors[...];\n      // Store in arrays\n      dummy.matrix.toArray(matrices, i * 16);\n      colors[i * 3] = color[0]; // R\n      colors[i * 3 + 1] = color[1]; // G\n      colors[i * 3 + 2] = color[2]; // B\n    }\n    return { matrices, colors };\n  }, [tasks, conflictIndices]);\n  \n  // Apply to mesh once mounted\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const mesh = meshRef.current;\n    for (let i = 0; i < tasks.count; i++) {\n      const matrix = new THREE.Matrix4();\n      matrix.fromArray(matrices, i * 16);\n      mesh.setMatrixAt(i, matrix);\n    }\n    mesh.instanceMatrix.needsUpdate = true;\n    mesh.instanceColor.array = colors;\n    mesh.instanceColor.needsUpdate = true;\n  }, [matrices, colors]);\n  \n  return <instancedMesh ref={meshRef} args={[geometry, material, tasks.count]} />;\n}\n```\n\n**Benefit**: 60k tasks rendered in single draw call; GPU-accelerated batching\n\n**Working Pattern: LOD Transitions with Smoothstep**\n\n```typescript\n// viewport.ts\nexport function getLODOpacity(zoom: number) {\n  const smoothstep = (edge0: number, edge1: number, x: number) => {\n    const t = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, (x - edge0) / (edge1 - edge0)));\n    return t * t * (3 - 2 * t); // Hermite interpolation\n  };\n  \n  let macro = 0, meso = 0, micro = 0;\n  \n  if (zoom < 0.425) {\n    macro = 1;\n  } else if (zoom < 0.575) {\n    // Crossfade zone (15% hysteresis)\n    macro = 1 - smoothstep(0.425, 0.575, zoom);\n    meso = smoothstep(0.425, 0.575, zoom);\n  } else if (zoom < 1.7) {\n    meso = 1;\n  } else if (zoom < 2.3) {\n    // Crossfade zone\n    meso = 1 - smoothstep(1.7, 2.3, zoom);\n    micro = smoothstep(1.7, 2.3, zoom);\n  } else {\n    micro = 1;\n  }\n  \n  return { macro, meso, micro };\n}\n```\n\n**Benefit**: Smooth crossfades between LOD layers; Hermite easing for visual polish\n\n**Anti-Pattern: Avoid**\n- ❌ useState in animation loops (stale closures)\n- ❌ useEffect for pan/zoom (update lag)\n- ❌ Array of Objects (cache miss locality)\n- ❌ Zustand for high-frequency updates (batching issues)\n- ❌ DOM rendering for 10k+ items (reflow/repaint)\n\n---\n\n## 4. USEFUL CODE PATTERNS & IMPLEMENTATIONS\n\n### 4.1 Viewport/Camera Management\n\n**Pattern**: World <-> Screen coordinate conversion\n```typescript\nexport function worldToScreen(\n  worldX: number, worldY: number, viewport: ViewportState\n): { x: number; y: number } {\n  const x = (worldX - viewport.x) * viewport.zoom + viewport.width / 2;\n  const y = (worldY - viewport.y) * viewport.zoom + viewport.height / 2;\n  return { x, y };\n}\n```\n\n**Usage**: Positioning UI overlays on canvas content\n\n### 4.2 Conflict Detection Algorithm\n\n```typescript\n// conflictDetection.ts\nexport function detectConflicts(tasks: TaskSoA): Conflict[] {\n  const conflicts: Conflict[] = [];\n  \n  for (let i = 0; i < tasks.count; i++) {\n    for (let j = i + 1; j < tasks.count; j++) {\n      // Same train, overlapping time?\n      if (tasks.trainIds[i] === tasks.trainIds[j]) {\n        const taskAEnd = tasks.startDays[i] + tasks.durations[i];\n        const taskBEnd = tasks.startDays[j] + tasks.durations[j];\n        \n        if (!(taskAEnd <= tasks.startDays[j] || taskBEnd <= tasks.startDays[i])) {\n          conflicts.push({ taskA: i, taskB: j });\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  return conflicts;\n}\n```\n\n### 4.3 Mock Data Generation (Deterministic)\n\n```typescript\n// mockData.ts\nfunction seededRandom(seed: number) {\n  return function () {\n    seed = (seed * 1103515245 + 12345) & 0x7fffffff;\n    return seed / 0x7fffffff;\n  };\n}\n\nexport function generateMockTasks(\n  trainCount: number = 128,\n  yearsSpan: number = 12,\n  tasksPerTrainPerYear: number = 4\n): Task[] {\n  const random = seededRandom(42); // Same seed = same data\n  // ... generate 128 * 12 * 4 ≈ 6k tasks\n}\n```\n\n**Benefit**: Reproducible test data across sessions\n\n### 4.4 Scenario Management (Sandbox Mode)\n\n```typescript\n// scenario.ts\ninterface ScenarioState {\n  mode: \"production\" | \"sandbox\";\n  modifications: Map<string, TaskModification>;\n  isDirty: boolean;\n}\n\nconst SCENARIO_COLORS = {\n  production: { label: \"Production\", accent: \"#0066cc\", bg: \"#0a1a3a\" },\n  sandbox: { label: \"Sandbox\", accent: \"#8b5cf6\", bg: \"#2d1b4e\" },\n};\n```\n\n**Pattern**: Track modifications separately, apply to canvas with conditional rendering\n\n### 4.5 PatternFly 6 Integration\n\n```typescript\n// App.tsx\nimport {\n  Masthead, MastheadBrand, Page, PageSection,\n  Toolbar, ToolbarGroup, ToolbarItem, Label, Button\n} from \"@patternfly/react-core\";\nimport { MinusIcon, PlusIcon } from \"@patternfly/react-icons\";\n\n// Consistent with design system tokens\n// Light/dark theme via data-theme attribute\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. REUSABLE PATTERNS FOR MAIN PROJECT\n\n### Immediately Reusable:\n\n1. **Viewport Store Pattern** (`stores/viewport.ts`)\n   - Camera position, zoom, bounds\n   - useSyncExternalStore pattern\n   - World ↔ screen coordinate conversion\n\n2. **Structure of Arrays (SoA)** (`utils/mockData.ts`)\n   - Per-instance color via InstancedBufferAttribute\n   - Per-instance transforms via matrix array\n\n4. **LOD System** (`viewport.ts`)\n   - Smooth crossfade transitions (Hermite smoothstep)\n   - Hysteresis zones to prevent flicker\n   - Three LOD levels: MACRO/MESO/MICRO\n\n5. **Conflict Detection** (`utils/conflictDetection.ts`)\n   - O(n²) scan for time-overlapping tasks on same train\n   - Efficient for 60k tasks in mock scenario\n\n6. **Design System** (`design-system.md`)\n   - CSS custom properties for theming\n   - Color palette with semantic tokens\n   - Spacing and typography scales\n\n7. **Harness System** (`progress.txt`, `features.json`)\n   - Session continuity tracking\n   - Feature passing/failing status\n   - Multi-phase sprint organization\n\n### Strategic Insights:\n\n1. **Never trust DOM rendering** for 10k+ items (use WebGL/canvas)\n2. **External stores** (not hooks) for animation loop synchronization\n3. **Separate data structure** from rendering (SoA separate from Three.js)\n4. **Competitor analysis** reveals genuine user needs (Marey charts, resource histograms)\n5. **Domain unknowns** (statutory tasks, bay limits, disruption mode) require proactive research\n6. **3-layer sandwich** (engine/canvas/HUD) keeps concerns cleanly separated\n7. **LOD with hysteresis** prevents jarring transitions during continuous zoom\n\n---\n\n## CONCLUSION\n\nThe mms-last-attempt project represents a **mature reference implementation** with:\n\n- ✅ **Comprehensive UX research** (competitor analysis + 10 unknown unknowns)\n- ✅ **Production code patterns** (SoA, InstancedMesh, external stores)\n- ✅ **Complete design system** (colors, typography, spacing, animations)\n- ✅ **Proven tech stack** (React 19, PatternFly 6, R3F 9, @belt/tools)\n- ✅ **Harness methodology** (session continuity, feature tracking)\n- ✅ **Critical domain insights** (statutory tasks, depot bays, KPIs, disruption mode)\n\n**Reusable in main project:**\n- Viewport store and camera management\n- Structure of Arrays data pattern\n- InstancedMesh rendering optimization\n- LOD system with smoothstep transitions\n- Design system tokens and theming\n- Conflict detection algorithm\n- Harness state tracking approach"

Uses InstancedMesh + d3-scale-chromatic for yellow→orange→red gradient\n- **MesoLayer** (Task Blocks): Visible at zoom 0.5-2.0. InstancedMesh for all task blocks with conflict indicators\n- **MicroLayer** (Detailed Cards): Visible at zoom > 2.0. HTML overlays with task details, grid lines, labels\n\n**State Management**: `state/`\n- `canvas-machine.ts`: Creates state machine with two slices (viewport, interaction)\n- `viewport.ts`: Camera position, momentum, animation, canvas size\n- `interaction.ts`: Hover/selection/focus state for tasks\n- Uses `@zazcart/tools` with `metadata: false` for 60fps optimization\n\n### 2.3 Data & Types\n\n**Mock Data Generator** (`data/generator.ts`):\n- 50 trains (30 ALSTOM, 20 KINKI Sharyo)\n- 10 years of tasks per train\n- ~8-12 tasks per train per year\n- ~5% have conflict flags\n- Generated on-demand (no persistence)\n\n**Domain Types** (`data/types.ts`):\n- `Train`: id, name, assetType\n- `Task`: id, trainId, startDate, endDate, type, hasConflict, predecessorId\n- `TaskRender`: Computed positions (trainIndex, startDay, duration, color)\n- `WorldBounds`: Navigation limits\n- `ViewConfig`: Pixel scales (pxPerDay=10, pxPerTrain=24)\n\n---\n\n## 3. STATE MANAGEMENT IMPLEMENTATION (@zazcart/tools)\n\n### 3.1 Usage Pattern\n\n```typescript\n// canvas-machine.ts\nexport const canvasMachine = createMachine({\n  id: 'canvas',\n  slices: {\n    viewport: viewportSlice,      // Camera, momentum, animation\n    interaction: interactionSlice, // Hover, selection, focus\n  },\n  metadata: false, // ⚠️ CRITICAL: Disables metadata tracking for 60fps\n});\n\n// Component access\nconst useCanvas = canvasMachine.useMachine;\nconst useCanvasSelector = canvasMachine.useSelector;\nconst canvasStore = { getState, dispatch, subscribe };\n```\n\n### 3.2 Viewport Slice (viewport.ts)\n\n**State**:\n- `camera`: { x, y } - world coordinates\n- `canvasSize`: { width, height }\n- `isInitialized`: boolean\n- `momentum`: { velocityX, velocityY, isActive }\n- `animation`: { isAnimating, startTime, duration, startX/Y/Zoom, targetX/Y/Zoom }\n- `isPanning`: boolean\n- Pan start/camera positions\n\n**Reducers**:\n- `setCamera(pos)`, `setCameraX(x)`, `setCameraY(y)`\n- `setCanvasSize(size)`\n- `initialize({ camera, canvasSize })`\n- `startMomentum`, `updateMomentum`, `stopMomentum`\n- `startAnimation`, `updateAnimation`, `stopAnimation`\n- `startPan`, `updatePan`, `endPan`\n- `reset()`\n\n### 3.3 Interaction Slice (interaction.ts)\n\n**State**:\n- `hoveredTaskId`: string | null (F018)\n- `mouseWorldPos`: { x, y } | null\n- `selectedTaskId`: string | null (F019)\n- `focusedTaskId`: string | null (F021 - keyboard navigation)\n- `isHoverable`: boolean\n\n**Reducers**:\n- `setHoveredTask(id)`, `clearHover()`\n- `setSelectedTask(id)`, `clearSelection()`\n- `setFocusedTask(id)`, `clearFocus()`\n- `setMouseWorldPos(pos)`\n- `reset()`\n\n---\n\n## 4. CANVAS/R3F IMPLEMENTATION\n\n### 4.1 LOD System\n\n**Three-Layer Architecture** with smooth blending:\n\n| LOD | Zoom | Render Method | Visibility |\n|-----|------|---------------|-----------|\n| **MACRO** | < 0.5x | Heatmap (InstancedMesh) | Strategic overview - monthly cells |\n| **MESO** | 0.5-2.0x | Task blocks (InstancedMesh) | Default view - DNA pattern |\n| **MICRO** | > 2.0x | Detail cards (Html) | Detailed inspection - labels, grid |\n\n**Blend Zones** (±0.15 around thresholds):\n- MACRO → MESO at 0.35-0.65 zoom\n- MESO → MICRO at 1.85-2.15 zoom\n- Smooth opacity transitions between layers\n\n**Implementation**:\n- `calculateLayerOpacities(zoom)` → { macro, meso, micro } opacities\n- `LODLayers` component renders all visible layers with interpolated opacity\n- Each layer controls its own visibility/culling\n\n### 4.2 Performance Optimizations\n\n1. **InstancedMesh Pre-allocation** (PERF-001):\n   - Single draw call per layer (instead of 1000s)\n   - Pre-allocate 100k instances max\n   - Use `mesh.instanceMatrix.needsUpdate` for dynamic updates\n\n2. **Viewport Culling** (PERF-002):\n   - RBushSpatialIndex for O(log n) queries\n   - `calculateViewportBounds()` expands render viewport slightly\n   - MicroLayer: `filterVisibleTasks()` reduces HTML elements\n   - Limit to 50 HTML labels in MicroLayer\n\n3. **Object Pooling**:\n   - Reuse Object3D temp objects in loops\n   - Avoid allocations in animation loops\n\n4. **GC Avoidance**:\n   - `@zazcart/tools` configured with `metadata: false`\n   - Prevents object allocations on every dispatch\n   - Direct state mutations (Immer-based)\n\n### 4.3 Interaction Handling\n\n**Pan**:\n- Mouse drag updates camera position\n- Bounds-checked to world limits\n- Momentum physics option (currently disabled - BUG-008)\n\n**Zoom**:\n- Scroll wheel (Google Maps-style)\n- Trackpad pinch support (with workarounds for BUG-009)\n- Zoom centered on cursor position\n- Smooth animation (250ms) vs direct application (trackpad)\n\n**Gestures**:\n- Keyboard: Arrow keys for pan, +/- for zoom (F027, F028)\n- Click: Select tasks (F019)\n- Hover: Highlight tasks + tooltip (F018, F020)\n- Keyboard focus: Navigate tasks (F021)\n\n---\n\n## 5. DATA FLOW SUMMARY\n\n```\nMock Data Generator\n    ↓\n    └→ Train[], Task[] (domain types)\n        ↓\n        └→ getRenderData() → TaskRender[] (computed positions)\n            ↓\n            ├→ RBush Spatial Index (world bounds)\n            │   ↓\n            │   Viewport Culling (visible tasks only)\n            │\n            ├→ MacroLayer (heatmap, if zoom < 0.5)\n            ├→ MesoLayer (blocks, if zoom 0.5-2.0)\n            └→ MicroLayer (details, if zoom > 2.0)\n                ↓\n                All layers pass state → @zazcart/tools (hover, select, focus)\n                ↓\n                Components re-render on state changes\n```\n\n---\n\n## 17. `bp6-monospace-text`\n```\n\n---\n\n## Phase 5: Archive Stale Documentation\n\n### 5.1 Move to Archive\n```\ndocs/RESEARCH.md → docs/archive/RESEARCH.md\ndocs/PARALLEL_EXECUTION.md → Was planned for Phase 3 of STATE-ARCH-001 but never integrated\n- Current generator.ts produces TaskRender[] directly consumed by layers\n- App runs at 120fps without it\n\n### 2.2 Delete Genesis Logs\n```bash\nrm -rf genesis/\n```\n\n**Rationale:** 6.9MB of old conversation logs, not needed.\n\n### 2.3 Remove Unused Dependencies\nEdit `apps/canvas/package.json`:\n\n**REMOVE from dependencies:**\n- `d3-selection` (not imported)\n- `d3-zoom` (R3F handles zoom, d3-zoom not used)\n- `troika-three-utils` (not imported)\n\n**REMOVE from devDependencies:**\n- `@types/d3-selection`\n- `@types/d3-zoom`\n\n### 2.4 Remove Stale Comments\nFiles with PatternFly references to clean:\n- `apps/canvas/src/canvas/InfiniteCanvas.tsx` (lines 13-14)\n- `apps/canvas/src/components/TimelineHeader.tsx` (line 13)\n\n---\n\n## Phase 3: Port UX Research from Reference\n\n### 3.1 Create UX Documentation Structure\n```\ndocs/\n├── ux/\n│   ├── _memory/design-system.md\n│   ├── screens.md                # From _memory/ux-screens.md\n│   ├── charts.md                 # From _memory/ux-charts.md\n│   └── navigation-flows.md       # From               # Old/stale docs\n    ├── RESEARCH.md\n    └── PARALLEL_EXECUTION.md\n```\n\n### 3.2 Adapt References to Current Stack\nWhen porting, update:\n- PatternFly 6 → BlueprintJS 6\n- React 19 → React 18\n- R3F 9 → R3F 8\n- @belt/tools → @zazcart/tools\n\n---\n\n## Phase 4: Design System Enforcement\n\n### 4.1 Create Design System Hook\n**File:** `.claude/hooks/enforce-design-system.sh`\n\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n# Enforce BlueprintJS design system\n# Block: custom colors, non-BP components, arbitrary spacing\n\nBLOCKED_PATTERNS=(\n  \"style={{.*color:\"\n  \"style={{.*background:\"\n  \"import.*from.*@patternfly\"\n  \"import.*from.*@mui\"\n  \"import.*from.*antd\"\n)\n\nfor pattern in \"${BLOCKED_PATTERNS[@]}\"; do\n  if grep -rE \"$pattern\" apps/canvas/src/ 2>/dev/null; then\n    echo \"BLOCKED: Design system violation - use BlueprintJS tokens\"\n    exit 1\n  fi\ndone\n```\n\n### 4.2 Update CLAUDE.md with Design System Section\n\nAdd section:\n```markdown\n## Design System (BlueprintJS 6)\n\n### Color Usage\n- Use Blueprint Intent colors: PRIMARY, SUCCESS, WARNING, DANGER\n- Dark theme tokens: `bp6-dark` class\n- Task types: PREVENT (green), CORRECT (orange), OVERHAUL (red)\n\n### Component Mapping\n| Need | BlueprintJS Component |\n|------|----------------------|\n| Navbar | `<Navbar>` + `<NavbarGroup>` |\n| Sidebar | `<Card>` with elevation |\n| Buttons | `<Button>` / `<ButtonGroup>` |\n| Tags | `<Tag>` with intent |\n| Panels | `<Card>` / `<Drawer>` |\n| Inputs | `<InputGroup>` |\n| Selects | `<Select>` / `<HTMLSelect>` |\n\n### Spacing Scale (4px base)\n- xs: 4px, sm: 8px, md: 12px, lg: 16px, xl: 24px\n\n### Typography\n- Use Blueprint's built-in typography classes\n- Monospace for train IDs: `bp6-monospace-text`\n```\n\n---\n\n## Phase 5: Archive Stale Documentation\n\n### 5.1 Move to Archive\n```\ndocs/RESEARCH.md → docs/archive/RESEARCH.md\ndocs/PARALLEL_EXECUTION.md → docs/archive/PARALLEL_EXECUTION.md\n```\n\n### 5.2 Keep Active Docs\n- `docs/SPECIFICATION.md` (authoritative spec)\n- `docs/MMS_COMPLETE_SPECIFICATION.md` (extended reference)\n- `docs/DOMAIN.md` (domain model)\n- `docs/UX_SPECIFICATION.md` (UX spec)\n- `docs/PERFORMANCE_LOGGING.md` (perf protocol)\n- `docs/QA_PROTOCOL.md` (testing protocol)\n\n---\n\n## Phase 6: Verification\n\n### 6.1 Pre-verification\n```bash\ncd apps/canvas\nbun install  # Ensure deps are updated after package.json changes\nbun run build  # Verify no import errors\n```\n\n### 6.2 Visual Verification (Playwright MCP)\n1. Navigate to http://localhost:5173\n2. Check console for errors\n3. Verify MACRO layer (zoom out < 0.5)\n4. Verify MESO layer (zoom 0.5-2.0)\n5. Verify MICRO layer (zoom > 2.0)\n6. Test pan/zoom interactions\n7. Verify 60fps+ in perf monitor\n\n### 6.3 Post-verification Commit\n```bash\ngit add -A\ngit commit -m \"refactor: course correction - remove dead code, port UX research\n\n- Remove unused EntityStore module\n- Remove genesis conversation logs\n- Remove unused deps (d3-selection, d3-zoom, troika-three-utils)\n- Port UX research from mms-last-attempt reference\n- Reset harness files (progress.txt, features.json)\n- Add design system enforcement hooks\n- Archive stale documentation\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.5 <noreply@anthropic.com>\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## File Change Summary\n\n### DELETE\n- `apps/canvas/src/entity-store/` (entire directory - 4 files)\n- `genesis/` (entire directory)\n\n### CREATE\n- `docs/ux/competitor-analysis.md`\n- `docs/ux/unknown-unknowns.md`\n- `docs/ux/design-system.md`\n- `docs/ux/screens.md`\n- `docs/ux/charts.md`\n- `docs/ux/navigation-flows.md`\n- `docs/architecture-decisions.md`\n- `docs/code-patterns.md`\n- `docs/archive/` (directory)\n- `.harness/archive/` (directory)\n- `.claude/hooks/enforce-design-system.sh`\n\n### MOVE\n- `progress.txt` → `.harness/archive/progress-2026-01-09.txt`\n- `features.json` → `.harness/archive/features-2026-01-09.json`\n- `docs/RESEARCH.md` → `docs/archive/RESEARCH.md`\n- `docs/PARALLEL_EXECUTION.md` → `docs/archive/PARALLEL_EXECUTION.md`\n\n### UPDATE\n- `apps/canvas/package.json` (remove unused deps)\n- `apps/canvas/src/canvas/InfiniteCanvas.tsx` (remove stale comments)\n- `apps/canvas/src/components/TimelineHeader.tsx` (remove stale comments)\n- `CLAUDE.md` (add design system section)\n- `progress.txt` (fresh content)\n- `features.json` (fresh content)\n\n---\n\n## Success Criteria\n\nAfter completion:\n- [ ] EntityStore directory deleted\n- [ ] genesis/ directory deleted\n- [ ] Unused dependencies removed from package.json\n- [ ] bun install successful\n- [ ] bun run build successful (no import errors)\n- [ ] Dev server starts without errors\n- [ ] All 3 LOD layers render correctly\n- [ ] No console errors\n- [ ] 60fps+ maintained\n- [ ] UX docs ported to docs/ux/\n- [ ] Harness files reset and archived\n- [ ] Design system hooks in place\n- [ ] Git commit created\n\n---\n\n## Post-Correction Project State\n\nAfter this plan:\n1. **Clean codebase** -       "content": "# MMS V1.0 Progress Log\n\n## Project Overview\nMetro Mileage Management System - High-performance visualization for railway fleet maintenance planning.\n\n**Tech Stack (Committed):**\n- React 18.3.1 + Vite\n- React Three Fiber 8.17 + Three.js 0.170\n- BlueprintJS 6.1.0 (UI components)\n- @zazcart/tools (state management)\n- RBush (spatial indexing)\n\n---\n\n## 2026-01-09: Course Correction Session\n\n### Context\nProject underwent major course correction to:\n1. Remove dead code (EntityStore, genesis/, unused deps)\n2. Port UX research from mms-last-attempt reference\n3. Reset harness files for clean state\n4. Establish design system enforcement\n\n### What Was Cleaned\n- Removed `apps/canvas/src/entity-store/` (unused)\n- Removed `genesis/` directory (6.9MB old logs)\n- Removed unused deps: d3-selection, d3-zoom, troika-three-utils\n- Archived stale docs to `docs/archive/`\n\n### What Was Added\n- `docs/ux/` directory with research from reference project\n- Design system enforcement via hooks\n- Updated CLAUDE.md with design system section\n\n### State After Correction\n- Stack: React 18 + BlueprintJS 6 + R3F 8 + @zazcart/tools\n- Features: Core visualization complete\n- Performance: 120fps verified (exceeds 60fps target)\n- Documentation: Consolidated in docs/\n\n---\n\n## V1.0 Genesis Status\n\n### Completed Features\n- 3-tier Semantic Zoom (MACRO/MESO/MICRO)\n- 60fps Pan/Zoom with momentum\n- 50 trains x 10 years mock data\n- Conflict visualization (red indicators)\n- Train sidebar with navigation\n- Timeline header with date labels\n- Minimap navigation\n- Task hover/selection\n- Keyboard shortcuts (partial)\n- Accessibility (ARIA labels)\n\n### Remaining Work\n1. Keyboard zoom (+/-) implementation verification\n2. Keyboard pan (arrows) implementation verification\n3. Cross-browser testing (Chrome, Firefox, Safari)\n4. Mobile touch gestures (deferred to V1.1)\n\n---\n\n## Development Protocol\n\n### Before Each Session\n1. READ this progress.txt\n2. READ features.json\n3.     "content": "     1→# UX Competitor Analysis - Railway Maintenance Scheduling Software\n     2→\n     3→> **Last Updated**: 2026-01-08\n     4→> **Purpose**: Steal best ideas from competitors - \"Good artists copy, great artists steal\"\n     5→> **Sources**: Web research via Anthropic Claude\n     6→\n     7→---\n     8→\n     9→## 1. IBM Maximo Scheduler\n    10→\n    11→### Overview\n    12→IBM's enterprise asset management system, widely used in rail/metro operations including Dubai Metro.\n    13→\n    14→### Key UI Features\n    15→\n    16→#### Gantt Chart Capabilities\n    17→- **Drag-and-drop scheduling**: Modify and mass-update work orders directly in Gantt view\n    18→- **Task dependencies**: Visual critical path with float calculation\n    19→- **Resource histogram**: Below Gantt showing resource loading vs availability\n    20→- **Multiple views**: Day, week, month, quarter, year timeline views\n    21→- **PM forecasting**: Gantt view for preventive maintenance with easy drag-drop adjustments\n    22→\n    23→#### Planning Views\n    24→- **Graphical Scheduling**: Long to short term planning with Gantt + histogram\n    25→- **Work View & Assignment View**: Both Gantt-based for supervisors\n    26→- **Dispatch View**: Day calendar + map showing labor/crew assignments with travel time\n    27→\n    28→#### Railway-Specific Features\n    29→- **Consist management**: For railway assets\n    30→- **Dynamic segmentation**: For Railways, Roads, Pipelines\n    31→- **Repair facility assignment**: Short-term planning for garage/railway shed assignment\n    32→\n    33→### Prometheus Group Enhancement (for Maximo)\n    34→- **Four-quadrant Gantt layout**: Flexible view\n    35→- **Real-time capacity effects**: See resource impact instantly\n    36→- **Direct Edit or Mass Change**: For orders and operations\n    37→\n    38→### Weaknesses to Exploit\n    39→- Fragmented into role-based apps (our opportunity: unified interface)\n    40→- Struggles with 10k+ records (our target: 60fps with 60k tasks)\n    41→- Discrete day/week/month tabs (our advantage: continuous semantic zoom)\n    42→\n    43→---\n    44→\n    45→## 2. Railnova (Brussels, Belgium)\n    46→\n    47→### Overview\n    48→Fleet management + telematics for rail industry. Clients include Eurotunnel, Alstom, Lineas, SNCF, DB Cargo.\n    49→\n    50→### Products\n    51→\n    52→#### Railfleet (ECM Fleet Management)\n    53→- **Operational Dashboard**: All fleet info in one place\n    54→  - Asset status\n    55→  - Restrictions\n    56→  - Rolling stock location\n    57→  - Key telematic values\n    58→  - Events and availability notifications\n    59→\n    60→- **Planning Dashboard**: Complete overview of maintenance events\n    61→  - Event states: unplanned, planned, overdue, closed\n    62→  - Per-asset filtering\n    63→  - Bundle corrective + preventive into interventions\n    64→\n    65→- **Maintenance Planning Dashboard**:\n    66→  - Filter events by type\n    67→  - Schedule new maintenance interventions\n    68→  - Bundle based on open events\n    69→\n    70→- **Digital Train Logbook**:\n    71→  - Real-time tablet view for drivers\n    72→  - Train availability and condition\n    73→  - Operational status and restrictions\n    74→  - Recent events list\n    75→\n    76→#### Railgenius (Real-time Monitoring)\n    77→- **Live Monitoring Module**:\n    78→  - Real-time telematics from all assets\n    79→  - Color-coded values for anomaly detection\n    80→  - Predictive alerts via detection rules\n    81→\n    82→- **Telematics Data Dashboard**:\n    83→  - Historical and real-time data\n    84→  - Usage pattern analysis\n    85→  - Fault code occurrence reporting\n    86→\n    87→### Integration Capabilities\n    88→- Web services API\n    89→- IBM Maximo, MySQL Server, .Net, Oracle, SAP integration\n    90→\n    91→### UI Patterns to Steal\n    92→- Color-coded anomaly indicators (spot abnormal values instantly)\n    93→- Event state pipeline (unplanned → planned → overdue → closed)\n    94→- Digital logbook concept for train-level status\n    95→- Bundling corrective + preventive events\n    96→\n    97→---\n    98→\n    99→## 3. SignatureRail (UK, Modaxo Group)\n   100→\n   101→### Overview\n   102→Train timetable and resource planning since 1994. Global presence with TrainPlan flagship product.\n   103→\n   104→### TrainPlan Features\n   105→- Timetable generation considering all resources and constraints\n   106→- Optimize capacity\n   107→- Reduce vehicle and operator costs\n   108→- Improve services\n   109→\n   110→### User Testimonial (Metro-North Railroad)\n   111→> \"TrainPlan allows us to manage our data in an efficient manner allowing for safe and high performing service changes to be implemented as quickly as possible.\"\n   112→\n   113→### Marey Chart Visualization (Industry Gold Standard)\n   114→\n   115→#### What is a Marey Chart?\n   116→- Invented by Étienne-Jules Marey (1878) based on Mr. Ibry's method\n   117→- **Axes**: Distance (Y) vs Time (X)\n   118→- **Trains**: Diagonal lines - slope = speed\n   119→- **Direction**: Top-left to bottom-right (one direction), bottom-left to top-right (reverse)\n   120→- **Stops**: Horizontal sections indicate stop duration\n   121→- **Crossings**: Lines crossing = trains passing each other\n   122→\n   123→#### Why Marey Charts are Superior\n   124→- \"Far superior representation for finding late trains and understanding delay propagation\"\n   125→- Both time and space dimensions in compact form\n   126→- Used as cover of Tufte's \"The Visual Display of Quantitative Information\"\n   127→- Speed immediately visible from line slope\n   128→\n   129→#### Modern Implementations\n   130→- [D3.js Observable Example](https://observablehq.com/@d3/mareys-trains)\n   131→- [JointJS Demo](https://www.jointjs.com/demos/marey-chart)\n   132→- [Tableau Public](https://public.tableau.com/en-us/s/blog/2015/08/marey-inspired-path-train-schedule)\n   133→\n   134→### UI Patterns to Steal\n   135→- Marey chart for train scheduling visualization\n   136→- What-if scenario management\n   137→- Constraint-aware scheduling\n   138→\n   139→---\n   140→\n   141→## 4. Other Notable Competitors\n   142→\n   143→### PTV Visum\n   144→- **Scenario management**: Create and manage infrastructure modifications\n   145→- **Fleet planning**: Depot capacities, turning times, empty runs\n   146→- **Batch evaluation**: Compare scenarios programmatically\n   147→\n   148→### TBEST (Free Desktop Software)\n   149→- **GIS-based**: Integrates socio-economic, land use, transit network\n   150→- **Scenario planning**: True network-based future year simulation\n   151→\n   152→### AnyLogic\n   153→- **Simulation-based optimization**: Two-layer approach\n   154→- **What-if scenarios**: Assess economic effects of changes\n   155→- **Replacement service planning**: For scheduled shutdowns\n   156→\n   157→### Tractian CMMS\n   158→- **AI-driven workload balancing**: Eliminates scheduling conflicts\n   159→- **Real-time technician availability**: Auto task prioritization\n   160→- **Visual Scheduling**: Plan by technician, area, or shift\n   161→- **Overload detection**: See idle time instantly\n   162→\n   163→### FaultFixers\n   164→- **Drag-and-drop calendar**: Intuitive ticket assignment\n   165→- **Gantt Chart view**: See everyone's schedule at once\n   166→\n   167→---\n   168→\n   169→## 5. Transit Dashboard Best Practices\n   170→\n   171→### Real-World Examples\n   172→\n   173→#### WMATA (Washington Metro)\n   174→- **MetroPulse**: Real-time headway and schedule adherence\n   175→- **Trains in service**: Live count\n   176→- **Service Excellence Dashboard**: Rail, Bus, MetroAccess data\n   177→\n   178→#### CTE KPI Platform\n   179→- **Single pane of glass**: Track progress, spot trends\n   180→- **Automated API feeds**: Vehicle telematics integration\n   181→- **Custom data inputs**: Flexible reporting\n   182→\n   183→### Common Transit KPIs\n   184→- Miles driven\n   185→- Drop sequence\n   186→- Number of stops\n   187→- Arrival/departure times\n   188→- DOT reportable incidents\n   189→- Speeding incidents\n   190→- Cost-per-mile\n   191→- Revenue-per-mile\n   192→- Miles per gallon\n   193→- Vehicle idle time\n   194→- On-time performance\n   195→- Missed trips\n   196→- Prediction accuracy\n   197→\n   198→---\n   199→\n   200→## 6. Gestalt Principles for Dashboard Design\n   201→\n   202→### Core Principles\n   203→\n   204→1. **Proximity**\n   205→   - Group related filters together\n   206→   - Place filter near its affected view\n   207→   - Example: Fleet status filters grouped with fleet list\n   208→\n   209→2. **Similarity**\n   210→   - Same colors for same data types\n   211→   - Consistent shapes for similar metrics\n   212→   - Example: All \"fit\" trains in green, all \"unfit\" in red\n   213→\n   214→3. **Enclosure**\n   215→   - Cards/boxes for related metrics\n   216→   - Clear distinction between data sets\n   217→   - Example: KPI cards with distinct borders\n   218→\n   219→4. **Connectedness**\n   220→   - Lines linking related elements\n   221→   - Network and line graph patterns\n   222→   - Example: Dependency lines between tasks\n   223→\n   224→5. **Closure**\n   225→   - Minimal axis lines (just X and Y enough)\n   226→   - User perceives complete structure\n   227→   - Example: Bar charts without full enclosure\n   228→\n   229→6. **Continuity**\n   230→   - Sort bars large to small\n   231→   - Time charts past to future\n   232→   - Perceived as continuous whole\n   233→\n   234→### Application to MMS\n   235→- Group maintenance metrics together (proximity)\n   236→- Color-code by fleet type and task status (similarity)\n   237→- Use cards for KPIs with clear borders (enclosure)\n   238→- Show task dependencies with connecting lines (connectedness)\n   239→- Minimal chart decoration (closure)\n   240→- Chronological timeline (continuity)\n   241→\n   242→---\n   243→\n   244→## 7. Calendar Heatmap Patterns\n   245→\n   246→### When to Use\n   247→- Daily values are important\n   248→- Want to view whole year at once\n   249→- Spot patterns at month/week/day level\n   250→- Compare weekdays vs weekends\n   251→\n   252→### When NOT to Use\n   253→- Need trend/seasonality analysis (use line charts)\n   254→- Monthly/yearly aggregate trends\n   255→- Simple KPI tracking\n   256→\n   257→### Best Practices\n   258→- Choose readable colors even with dark shades\n   259→- Use continuous date calendar table\n   260→- Common layouts: 4x3, 3x4, 6x2 grids\n   261→- Color intensity = value magnitude\n   262→\n   263→### MMS Application\n   264→- **MACRO view**: Calendar heatmap showing maintenance density\n   265→- **Color scale**: Viridis (low=yellow → high=purple)\n   266→- **Drill-down**: Click month/week to zoom MESO level\n   267→\n   268→---\n   269→\n   270→## 8. MMS Differentiators (vs Competitors)\n   271→\n   272→| Feature | Competitors | MMS |\n   273→|---------|-------------|-----|\n   274→| Zoom | Discrete tabs (day/week/month) | Continuous semantic zoom |\n   275→| Performance | Maximo struggles at 10k | 60fps with 60k tasks |\n   276→| Interface | Fragmented role-based apps | Unified single canvas |\n   277→| Conflict resolution | Manual identification | Visual drag-drop with instant feedback |\n   278→| Scenario mode | Separate planning modules | Inline sandbox with violet visual |\n   279→| Chart type | Gantt only | Gantt + Marey + Heatmap (LOD) |\n   280→\n   281→---\n   282→\n   283→## 9. Features to Steal (Priority Order)\n   284→\n   285→### HIGH PRIORITY\n   286→1. Drag-and-drop Gantt scheduling (IBM Maximo, Tractian)\n   287→2. Color-coded anomaly indicators (Railnova)\n   288→3. Event state pipeline (unplanned → planned → overdue → closed)\n   289→4. Resource histogram below schedule (Maximo)\n   290→5. Marey chart for train visualization (SignatureRail)\n   291→\n   292→### MEDIUM PRIORITY\n   293→6. Digital train logbook per asset (Railnova)\n   294→7. Four-quadrant flexible layout (Prometheus)\n   295→8. Scenario comparison with batch evaluation (PTV Visum)\n   296→9. What-if scenario with economic impact (AnyLogic)\n   297→10. Calendar heatmap for maintenance density\n   298→\n   299→### FUTURE CONSIDERATION\n   300→11. AI-driven workload balancing (Tractian)\n   301→12. GIS integration (TBEST)\n   302→13. Predictive maintenance alerts (Railgenius)\n   303→14. Mobile dispatch interface (Railnova)\n   304→\n   305→---\n   306→\n   307→## Sources\n   308→\n   309→- [IBM Maximo Scheduler - Prometheus Group](https://www.prometheusgroup.com/solutions/planning-and-scheduling-ibm-maximo)\n   310→- [Railnova Official Site](https://www.railnova.eu/)\n   311→- [Railfleet ECM Platform](https://www.railnova.eu/products/railfleet/)\n   312→- [SignatureRail Planning Solutions](https://signaturerail.com/planning-solutions/)\n   313→- [Marey's Trains - D3 Observable](https://observablehq.com/@d3/mareys-trains)\n   314→- [Gestalt Principles in Dashboard Design](https://playfairdata.com/applying-gestalt-principles-to-dashboard-design/)\n   315→- [WMATA Service Excellence Dashboard](https://www.wmata.com/initiatives/open-data-hub/Metro-Service-Excellence-Dashboard.cfm)\n   316→- [Tractian CMMS](https://tractian.com/en/cmms/planning-and-scheduling)\n   317→- [PTV Visum](https://www.ptvgroup.com/en-us/products/ptv-visum)\n   318→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.       "new_string": "## BlueprintJS 6 Integration Notes\n\n- Use BlueprintJS 6 tokens where available (bp6-* CSS classes)\n- Override with `--mms-*` tokens for custom values\n- Cards use `Elevation.TWO` shadow via `<Card elevation={2}>`\n- Drawers use `<Drawer>` component, position on right for task details\n- Maintain dark theme via `bp6-dark` class on root\n- Use Intent colors: PRIMARY, SUCCESS, WARNING, DANGER\n\n### BlueprintJS Component Mapping\n\n| UI Need | BlueprintJS Component |\n|---------|----------------------|\n| Navbar | `<Navbar>` + `<NavbarGroup>` |\n| Sidebar | `<Card>` with elevation |\n| Buttons | `<Button>` / `<ButtonGroup>` |\n| Tags/Labels | `<Tag>` with intent |\n| Panels | `<Card>` / `<Drawer>` |\n| Inputs | `<InputGroup>` |\n| Selects | `<Select>` / `<HTMLSelect>` |\n| Tooltips | `<Tooltip>` |\n| Toasts | `<OverlayToaster>` |"
    }
